# Docker container RUN

<h1 class="scroll-mt-36">docker container run</h1><table><tbody><tr><th class="text-left w-32">Description</th><td>Create and run a new container from an image</td></tr><tr><th class="text-left data-tooltip-body="" class="absolute left-0 top-0 hidden max-w-56 rounded bg-accent-light p-2 text-white dark:bg-accent-dark" role="tooltip">An alias is a short or memorable alternative for a longer command.<div data-tooltip-arrow="" class="absolute h-2 w-2 rotate-45 bg-accent-light dark:bg-accent-dark"></div></div></div></th><td><div class="flex gap-3"><code>docker run</code></div></td></tr></tbody></table><h2 class="scroll-mt-20" id="description"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#description">Description</a></h2><p>The <code>docker run</code> command runs a command in a new container, pulling the image if needed and starting the container.</p><p>You can restart a stopped container with all its previous changes intact using <code>docker start</code>.
Use <code>docker ps -a</code> to view a list of all containers, including those that are stopped.</p><h2 class="scroll-mt-20" id="options"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#options">Options</a></h2><table><thead><tr><th>Option</th><th>Default</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><a class="link" href="#add-host"><code>--add-host</code></a></td><td></td><td>Add a custom host-to-IP mapping (host:ip)</td></tr><tr><td><code>--annotation</code></td><td></td><td><span class="not-prose px-1 rounded-sm bg-blue-light dark:bg-blue-dark text-white text-xs">API 1.43+</span>
Add an annotation to the container (passed through to the OCI runtime)<br></td></tr><tr><td><a class="link" href="#attach"><code>-a, --attach</code></a></td><td></td><td>Attach to STDIN, STDOUT or STDERR</td></tr><tr><td><code>--blkio-weight</code></td><td></td><td>Block IO (relative weight), between 10 and 1000, or 0 to disable (default 0)<br></td></tr><tr><td><code>--blkio-weight-device</code></td><td></td><td>Block IO weight (relative device weight)</td></tr><tr><td><code>--cap-add</code></td><td></td><td>Add Linux capabilities</td></tr><tr><td><code>--cap-drop</code></td><td></td><td>Drop Linux capabilities</td></tr><tr><td><a class="link" href="#cgroup-parent"><code>--cgroup-parent</code></a></td><td></td><td>Optional parent cgroup for the container</td></tr><tr><td><code>--cgroupns</code></td><td></td><td><span class="not-prose px-1 rounded-sm bg-blue-light dark:bg-blue-dark text-white text-xs">API 1.41+</span>
Cgroup namespace to use (host|private)<br>'host': Run the container in the Docker host's cgroup namespace<br>'private': Run the container in its own private cgroup namespace<br>'': Use the cgroup namespace as configured by the<br>default-cgroupns-mode option on the daemon (default)</td></tr><tr><td><a class="link" href="#cidfile"><code>--cidfile</code></a></td><td></td><td>Write the container ID to the file</td></tr><tr><td><code>--cpu-count</code></td><td></td><td>CPU count (Windows only)</td></tr><tr><td><code>--cpu-percent</code></td><td></td><td>CPU percent (Windows only)</td></tr><tr><td><code>--cpu-period</code></td><td></td><td>Limit CPU CFS (Completely Fair Scheduler) period</td></tr><tr><td><code>--cpu-quota</code></td><td></td><td>Limit CPU CFS (Completely Fair Scheduler) quota</td></tr><tr><td><code>--cpu-rt-period</code></td><td></td><td><span class="not-prose px-1 rounded-sm bg-blue-light dark:bg-blue-dark text-white text-xs">API 1.25+</span>
Limit CPU real-time period in microseconds</td></tr><tr><td><code>--cpu-rt-runtime</code></td><td></td><td><span class="not-prose px-1 rounded-sm bg-blue-light dark:bg-blue-dark text-white text-xs">API 1.25+</span>

Number of CPUs</td></tr><tr><td><code>--cpuset-cpus</code></td><td></td><td>CPUs in which to allow execution (0-3, 0,1)</td></tr><tr><td><code>--cpuset-mems</code></td><td></td><td>MEMs in which to allow execution (0-3, 0,1)</td></tr><tr><td><a class="link" href="#detach"><code>-d, --detach</code></a></td><td></td><td>Run container in background and print container ID</td></tr><tr><td><a GPU devices to add to the container ('all' to pass all GPUs)</td></tr><tr><td><code>--group-add</code></td><td></td><td>Add additional groups to join</td></tr><tr><td><code>--health-cmd</code></td><td></td><td>Command to run to check health</td></tr><tr><td><code>--health-interval</code></td><td></td><td>Time between running the check (ms|s|m|h) (default 0s)</td></tr><tr><td><code>--health-retries</code></td><td></td><td>Consecutive failures needed to report unhealthy</td></tr><tr><td><code>--health-start-interval</code></td><td></td><td><span class="not-prose px-1 rounded-sm bg-blue-light dark:bg-blue-dark text-white text-xs">API 1.44+</span>

The
following example runs a container named <code>test</code> using the <code>nginx:alpine</code> image
in
<a class="link" href="#detach">detached mode</a>.</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC0tbmFtZSB0ZXN0IC1kIG5naW54OmFscGluZQo0YmVkNzZkM2FkNDI4Yjg4OWM1NmMxZWNjMmJmMmVkOTVjYjA4MjU2ZGIyMmRjNWVmNTg2M2UxZDAzMjUyYTE5CiQgZG9ja2VyIHBzCkNPTlRBSU5FUiBJRCAgIElNQUdFICAgICAgICAgIENPTU1BTkQgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICBDUkVBVEVEICAgICAgICBTVEFUVVMgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICBQT1JUUyAgICAgTkFNRVMKNGJlZDc2ZDNhZDQyICAgbmdpbng6YWxwaW5lICAgIi9kb2NrZXItZW50cnlwb2ludC7igKYiICAgMSBzZWNvbmQgYWdvICAgVXAgTGVzcyB0aGFuIGEgc2Vjb25kICAgODAvdGNwICAgIHRlc3Q=', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));

<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run --name <span class="nb">test</span> -d nginx:alpine
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">4bed76d3ad428b889c56c1ecc2bf2ed95cb08256db22dc5ef5863e1d03252a19

</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">CONTAINER ID   IMAGE          COMMAND                  CREATED        STATUS                  PORTS     NAMES
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">4bed76d3ad42   nginx:alpine   "/docker-entrypoint.â€¦"   1 second ago   Up Less than a second   80/tcp    test
</span></span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>You can reference the container by name with other commands. For example, the
following commands stop and remove a container named <code>test</code>:</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgc3RvcCB0ZXN0CnRlc3QKJCBkb2NrZXIgcm0gdGVzdAp0ZXN0', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));

<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker stop <span class="nb">test</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">test
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go"></span><span class="gp">$</span> docker rm <span class="nb">test</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">test
</span></span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>If you don't specify a custom name using the <code>--name</code> flag, the daemon assigns
a randomly generated name, such as <code>vibrant_cannon</code>, to the container. Using a
custom-defined name provides the benefit of having an easy-to-remember ID for a
container.</p><p>Moreover, if you connect the container to a user-defined bridge network, other
containers on the same network can refer to the container by name via DNS.</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgbmV0d29yayBjcmVhdGUgbXluZXQKY2I3OWY0NTk0OGQ4N2UzODllMTIwMTNmYTRkOTY5Njg5ZWQyYzMzMTY5ODVkZDgzMmE0M2FhZWM5YTBmZTM5NAokIGRvY2tlciBydW4gLS1uYW1lIHRlc3QgLS1uZXQgbXluZXQgLWQgbmdpbng6YWxwaW5lCjU4ZGY2ZWNmYmMyYWQ3YzQyZDA4OGVkMDI4ZDM2N2Y5ZTIyYTVmODM0ZDdjNzRjNjZjMGFiMDQ4NTYyNmMzMmEKJCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC0tbmV0IG15bmV0IGJ1c3lib3g6bGF0ZXN0IHBpbmcgdGVzdApQSU5HIHRlc3QgKDE3Mi4xOC4wLjIpOiA1NiBkYXRhIGJ5dGVzCjY0IGJ5dGVzIGZyb20gMTcyLjE4LjAuMjogc2VxPTAgdHRsPTY0IHRpbWU9MC4wNzMgbXMKNjQgYnl0ZXMgZnJvbSAxNzIuMTguMC4yOiBzZXE9MSB0dGw9NjQgdGltZT0wLjQxMSBtcwo2NCBieXRlcyBmcm9tIDE3Mi4xOC4wLjI6IHNlcT0yIHR0bD02NCB0aW1lPTAuMzE5IG1zCjY0IGJ5dGVzIGZyb20gMTcyLjE4LjAuMjogc2VxPTMgdHRsPTY0IHRpbWU9MC4zODMgbXMKLi4u', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));

file of your choosing. This is similar to how some programs might write out
their process ID to a file (you might've seen them as PID files):</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC0tY2lkZmlsZSAvdG1wL2RvY2tlcl90ZXN0LmNpZCB1YnVudHUgZWNobyAidGVzdCI=', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));

</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>This creates a container and prints <code>test</code> to the console. The <code>cidfile</code>
flag makes Docker attempt to create a new file and write the container ID to it.
If the file exists already, Docker returns an error. Docker closes this
file when <code>docker run</code> exits.</p><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="pid"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#pid">PID settings (--pid)</a></h3><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'LS1waWQ9IiIgIDogU2V0IHRoZSBQSUQgKFByb2Nlc3MpIE5hbWVzcGFjZSBtb2RlIGZvciB0aGUgY29udGFpbmVyLAogICAgICAgICAgICAgJ2NvbnRhaW5lcjo8bmFtZXxpZD4nOiBqb2lucyBhbm90aGVyIGNvbnRhaW5lcidzIFBJRCBuYW1lc3BhY2UKICAgICAgICAgICAgICdob3N0JzogdXNlIHRoZSBob3N0J3MgUElEIG5hbWVzcGFjZSBpbnNpZGUgdGhlIGNvbnRhaW5lcg==', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-text" data-lang="text"><span class="line"><span class="cl">--pid=""  : Set the PID (Process) Namespace mode for the container,
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">             'container:&lt;name|id&gt;': joins another container's PID namespace
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">             'host': use the host's PID namespace inside the container</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>By default, all containers have the PID namespace enabled.</p><p>PID namespace provides separation of processes. The PID Namespace removes the
view of the system processes, and allows process ids to be reused including
PID 1.</p><p>In certain cases you want your container to share the host's process namespace,
allowing processes within the container to see all of the processes on the
system. For example, you could build a container with debugging tools like
<code>strace</code> or <code>gdb</code>, but want to use these tools when debugging processes within
the container.</p><h4 class="scroll-mt-20" id="example-run-htop-inside-a-container"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#example-run-htop-inside-a-container">Example: run htop inside a container</a></h4><p>To run <code>htop</code> in a container that shares the process namespac of the host:</p><ol><li><p>Run an alpine container with the <code>--pid=host</code> option:</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC0tcm0gLWl0IC0tcGlkPWhvc3QgYWxwaW5l', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;

      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">

</span></span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></li></ol><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="userns"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#userns">Disable namespace remapping for a container (--userns)</a></h3><p>If you enable user namespaces on the daemon,
all containers are started with user namespaces enabled by default.
To disable user namespace remapping for a specific container,
you can set the <code>--userns</code> flag to <code>host</code>.</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'ZG9ja2VyIHJ1biAtLXVzZXJucz1ob3N0IGhlbGxvLXdvcmxk', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));

<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">docker run --userns=host hello-world
</span></span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p><code>host</code> is the only valid value for the <code>--userns</code> flag.</p><p>For more information, refer to
<a class="link" href="/engine/security/userns-remap/">Isolate containers with a user namespace</a>.</p><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="uts"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#uts">UTS settings (--uts)</a></h3><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'LS11dHM9IiIgIDogU2V0IHRoZSBVVFMgbmFtZXNwYWNlIG1vZGUgZm9yIHRoZSBjb250YWluZXIKICAgICAgICAgICAgJ2hvc3QnOiB1c2UgdGhlIGhvc3QncyBVVFMgbmFtZXNwYWNlIGluc2lkZSB0aGUgY29udGFpbmVy', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-text" data-lang="text"><span class="line"><span class="cl">--uts=""  : Set the UTS namespace mode for the container
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">            'host': use the host's UTS namespace inside the container</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>The UTS namespace is for setting the hostname and the domain that's visible to
running processes in that namespace. By default, all containers, including
those with <code>--network=host</code>, have their own UTS namespace. Setting <code>--uts</code> to
<code>host</code> results in the container using the same UTS namespace as the host.</p><blockquote><p><strong>Note</strong></p><p>Docker disallows combining the <code>--hostname</code> and <code>--domainname</code> flags with
<code>--uts=host</code>. This is to prevent containers running in the host's UTS
namespace from attempting to change the hosts' configuration.</p></blockquote><p>You may wish to share the UTS namespace with the host if you would like the
hostname of the container to change as the hostname of the host changes. A more
advanced use case would be changing the host's hostname from a container.</p><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="ipc"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#ipc">IPC settings (--ipc)</a></h3><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'LS1pcGM9Ik1PREUiICA6IFNldCB0aGUgSVBDIG1vZGUgZm9yIHRoZSBjb250YWluZXI=', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-text" data-lang="text"><span class="line"><span class="cl">--ipc="MODE"  : Set the IPC mode for the container</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>The <code>--ipc</code> flag accepts the following values:</p><table><thead><tr><th style="text-align:left">Value</th><th style="text-align:left">Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td style="text-align:left">""</td><td style="text-align:left">Use daemon's default.</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:left">"none"</td><td style="text-align:left">Own private IPC namespace, with /dev/shm not mounted.</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:left">"private"</td><td style="text-align:left">Own private IPC namespace.</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:left">"shareable"</td><td style="text-align:left">Own private IPC namespace, with a possibility to share it with other containers.</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:left">"container:&lt;<em>name-or-ID</em>&gt;"</td><td style="text-align:left">Join another ("shareable") container's IPC namespace.</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:left">"host"</td><td style="text-align:left">Use the host system's IPC namespace.</td></tr></tbody></table><p>If not specified, daemon default is used, which can either be <code>"private"</code>
or <code>"shareable"</code>, depending on the daemon version and configuration.</p><p><a class="link" href="https://linux.die.net/man/5/ipc" target="_blank" rel="noopener">System V interprocess communication (IPC)<span class="pl-1 icon-svg icon-sm"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M180-120q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-6e2q0-24 18-42t42-18h249q12.75.0 21.375 8.675 8.625 8.676 8.625 21.5.0 12.825-8.625 21.325T429-780H180v6e2h6e2v-249q0-12.75 8.675-21.375 8.676-8.625 21.5-8.625 12.825.0 21.325 8.625T840-429v249q0 24-18 42t-42 18H180zm6e2-617L403-360q-9 9-21 8.5t-21-9.5-9-21 9-21l377-377H549q-12.75.0-21.375-8.675-8.625-8.676-8.625-21.5.0-12.825 8.625-21.325T549-840h291v291q0 12.75-8.675 21.375-8.676 8.625-21.5 8.625-12.825.0-21.325-8.625T780-549v-188z"></path></svg></span></a>
namespaces provide separation of named shared memory segments, semaphores and
message queues.</p><p>Shared memory segments are used to accelerate inter-process communication at
memory speed, rather than through pipes or through the network stack. Shared
memory is commonly used by databases and custom-built (typically C/OpenMPI,
C++/using boost libraries) high performance applications for scientific
computing and financial services industries. If these types of applications
are broken into multiple containers, you might need to share the IPC mechanisms
of the containers, using <code>"shareable"</code> mode for the main (i.e. "donor")
container, and <code>"container:&lt;donor-name-or-ID&gt;"</code> for other containers.</p><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="privileged"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#privileged">Escalate container privileges (--privileged)</a></h3><p>The <code>--privileged</code> flag gives the following capabilities to a container:</p><ul><li>Enables all Linux kernel capabilities</li><li>Disables the default seccomp profile</li><li>Disables the default AppArmor profile</li><li>Disables the SELinux process label</li><li>Grants access to all host devices</li><li>Makes <code>/sys</code> read-write</li><li>Makes cgroups mounts read-write</li></ul><p>In other words, the container can then do almost everything that the host can
do. This flag exists to allow special use-cases, like running Docker within
Docker.</p><blockquote class="warning"><p><strong>Warning</strong></p><p>Use the <code>--privileged</code> flag with caution.
A container with <code>--privileged</code> is not a securely sandboxed process.
Containers in this mode can get a root shell on the host
and take control over the system.</p><p>For most use cases, this flag should not be the preferred solution.
If your container requires escalated privileges,
you should prefer to explicitly grant the necessary permissions,
for example by adding individual kernel capabilities with <code>--cap-add</code>.</p><p>For more information, see
<a class="link" href="/engine/reference/run/#runtime-privilege-and-linux-capabilities">Runtime privilege and Linux capabilities</a></p></blockquote><p>The following example doesn't work, because by default, Docker drops most
potentially dangerous kernel capabilities, including <code>CAP_SYS_ADMIN </code>(which is
required to mount filesystems).</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC10IC1pIC0tcm0gdWJ1bnR1IGJhc2gKcm9vdEBiYzMzODk0MmVmMjA6LyMgbW91bnQgLXQgdG1wZnMgbm9uZSAvbW50Cm1vdW50OiBwZXJtaXNzaW9uIGRlbmllZA==', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run -t -i --rm ubuntu bash
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">root@bc338942ef20:/# mount -t tmpfs none /mnt
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">mount: permission denied
</span></span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>It works when you add the <code>--privileged</code> flag:</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC10IC1pIC0tcHJpdmlsZWdlZCB1YnVudHUgYmFzaApyb290QDUwZTNmNTdlMTZlNjovIyBtb3VudCAtdCB0bXBmcyBub25lIC9tbnQKcm9vdEA1MGUzZjU3ZTE2ZTY6LyMgZGYgLWgKRmlsZXN5c3RlbSAgICAgIFNpemUgIFVzZWQgQXZhaWwgVXNlJSBNb3VudGVkIG9uCm5vbmUgICAgICAgICAgICAxLjlHICAgICAwICAxLjlHICAgMCUgL21udA==', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run -t -i --privileged ubuntu bash
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">root@50e3f57e16e6:/# mount -t tmpfs none /mnt
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">root@50e3f57e16e6:/# df -h
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">Filesystem      Size  Used Avail Use% Mounted on
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">none            1.9G     0  1.9G   0% /mnt
</span></span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="workdir"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#workdir">Set working directory (-w, --workdir)</a></h3><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC13IC9wYXRoL3RvL2Rpci8gLWkgLXQgdWJ1bnR1IHB3ZA==', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));

</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>The <code>-w</code> option runs the command executed inside the directory specified, in this example,
<code>/path/to/dir/</code>. If the path doesn't exist, Docker creates it inside the container.</p><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="storage-opt"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#storage-opt">Set storage driver options per container (--storage-opt)</a></h3><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC1pdCAtLXN0b3JhZ2Utb3B0IHNpemU9MTIwRyBmZWRvcmEgL2Jpbi9iYXNo', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));

<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run -it --storage-opt <span class="nv">size</span><span class="o">=</span>120G fedora /bin/bash
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>This (size) constraints the container filesystem size to 120G at creation time.
This option is only available for the <code>btrfs</code>, <code>overlay2</code>, <code>windowsfilter</code>,
and <code>zfs</code> storage drivers.</p><p>For the <code>overlay2</code> storage driver, the size option is only available if the
backing filesystem is <code>xfs</code> and mounted with the <code>pquota</code> mount option.
Under these conditions, you can pass any size less than the backing filesystem size.</p><p>For the <code>windowsfilter</code>, <code>btrfs</code>, and <code>zfs</code> storage drivers, you cannot pass a
size less than the Default BaseFS Size.</p><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="tmpfs"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#tmpfs">Mount tmpfs (--tmpfs)</a></h3><p>The <code>--tmpfs</code> flag lets you create a <code>tmpfs</code> mount.</p><p>The options that you can pass to <code>--tmpfs</code> are identical to the Linux <code>mount -t tmpfs -o</code> command. The following example mounts an empty <code>tmpfs</code> into the
container with the <code>rw</code>, <code>noexec</code>, <code>nosuid</code>, <code>size=65536k</code> options.</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC1kIC0tdG1wZnMgL3J1bjpydyxub2V4ZWMsbm9zdWlkLHNpemU9NjU1MzZrIG15X2ltYWdl', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));

</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>You can use volumes in combination with the <code>--read-only</code> flag to control where
a container writes files. The <code>--read-only</code> flag mounts the container's root
filesystem as read only prohibiting writes to locations other than the
specified volumes for the container.</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC10IC1pIC12IC92YXIvcnVuL2RvY2tlci5zb2NrOi92YXIvcnVuL2RvY2tlci5zb2NrIC12IC9wYXRoL3RvL3N0YXRpYy1kb2NrZXItYmluYXJ5Oi91c3IvYmluL2RvY2tlciBidXN5Ym94IHNo', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));

      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">

</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>By bind-mounting the Docker Unix socket and statically linked Docker

you give the container the full access to create and manipulate the host's

      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">

<a class="link" href="/storage/volumes/">manage data in containers</a></p><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="mount"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#mount">Add bind mounts or volumes using the --mount flag</a></h3><p>The <code>--mount</code> flag allows you to mount volumes, host-directories, and <code>tmpfs</code>
mounts in a container.</p><p>The <code>--mount</code> flag supports most options supported by the <code>-v</code> or the
<code>--volume</code> flag, but uses a different syntax. For in-depth information on the
<code>--mount</code> flag, and a comparison between <code>--volume</code> and <code>--mount</code>, refer to
<a class="link" href="/storage/bind-mounts/">Bind mounts</a>.</p><p>Even though there is no plan to deprecate <code>--volume</code>, usage of <code>--mount</code> is recommended.</p><p>Examples:</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC0tcmVhZC1vbmx5IC0tbW91bnQgdHlwZT12b2x1bWUsdGFyZ2V0PS9pY2Fud3JpdGUgYnVzeWJveCB0b3VjaCAvaWNhbndyaXRlL2hlcmU=', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));

      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">

<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run -t -i --mount <span class="nv">type</span><span class="o">=</span>bind,src<span class="o">=</span>/data,dst<span class="o">=</span>/data busybox sh
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="publish"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#publish">Publish or expose port (-p, --expose)</a></h3><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC1wIDEyNy4wLjAuMTo4MDo4MDgwL3RjcCBuZ2lueDphbHBpbmU=', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run -p 127.0.0.1:80:8080/tcp nginx:alpine
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>This binds port <code>8080</code> of the container to TCP port <code>80</code> on <code>127.0.0.1</code> of the
host. You can also specify <code>udp</code> and <code>sctp</code> ports. The
<a class="link" href="/network/">Networking overview
page</a> explains in detail how to publish ports
with Docker.</p><blockquote><p><strong>Note</strong></p><p>If you don't specify an IP address (i.e., <code>-p 80:80</code> instead of <code>-p 127.0.0.1:80:80</code>) when publishing a container's ports, Docker publishes the
port on all interfaces (address <code>0.0.0.0</code>) by default. These ports are
externally accessible. This also applies if you configured UFW to block this
specific port, as Docker manages its own iptables rules.
<a class="link" href="/network/packet-filtering-firewalls/">Read
more</a></p></blockquote><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC0tZXhwb3NlIDgwIG5naW54OmFscGluZQ==', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run --expose <span class="m">80</span> nginx:alpine
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>This exposes port <code>80</code> of the container without publishing the port to the host
system's interfaces.</p><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="publish-all"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#publish-all">Publish all exposed ports (-P, --publish-all)</a></h3><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC1QIG5naW54OmFscGluZQ==', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run -P nginx:alpine
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>The <code>-P</code>, or <code>--publish-all</code>, flag publishes all the exposed ports to the host.
Docker binds each exposed port to a random port on the host.</p><p>The <code>-P</code> flag only publishes port numbers that are explicitly flagged as
exposed, either using the Dockerfile <code>EXPOSE</code> instruction or the <code>--expose</code>
flag for the <code>docker run</code> command.</p><p>The range of ports are within an <em>ephemeral port range</em> defined by
<code>/proc/sys/net/ipv4/ip_local_port_range</code>. Use the <code>-p</code> flag to explicitly map a
single port or range of ports.</p><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="pull"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#pull">Set the pull policy (--pull)</a></h3><p>Use the <code>--pull</code> flag to set the image pull policy when creating (and running)
the container.</p><p>The <code>--pull</code> flag can take one of these values:</p><table><thead><tr><th style="text-align:left">Value</th><th style="text-align:left">Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td style="text-align:left"><code>missing</code> (default)</td><td style="text-align:left">Pull the image if it was not found in the image cache, or use the cached image otherwise.</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:left"><code>never</code></td><td style="text-align:left">Do not pull the image, even if it's missing, and produce an error if the image does not exist in the image cache.</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:left"><code>always</code></td><td style="text-align:left">Always perform a pull before creating the container.</td></tr></tbody></table><p>When creating (and running) a container from an image, the daemon checks if the
image exists in the local image cache. If the image is missing, an error is
returned to the CLI, allowing it to initiate a pull.</p><p>The default (<code>missing</code>) is to only pull the image if it's not present in the
daemon's image cache. This default allows you to run images that only exist
locally (for example, images you built from a Dockerfile, but that have not
been pushed to a registry), and reduces networking.</p><p>The <code>always</code> option always initiates a pull before creating the container. This
option makes sure the image is up-to-date, and prevents you from using outdated
images, but may not be suitable in situations where you want to test a locally
built image before pushing (as pulling the image overwrites the existing image
in the image cache).</p><p>The <code>never</code> option disables (implicit) pulling images when creating containers,
and only uses images that are available in the image cache. If the specified
image is not found, an error is produced, and the container is not created.
This option is useful in situations where networking is not available, or to
prevent images from being pulled implicitly when creating containers.</p><p>The following example shows <code>docker run</code> with the <code>--pull=never</code> option set,
which produces en error as the image is missing in the image-cache:</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC0tcHVsbD1uZXZlciBoZWxsby13b3JsZApkb2NrZXI6IEVycm9yIHJlc3BvbnNlIGZyb20gZGFlbW9uOiBObyBzdWNoIGltYWdlOiBoZWxsby13b3JsZDpsYXRlc3Qu', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">

</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>Use the <code>-e</code>, <code>--env</code>, and <code>--env-file</code> flags to set simple (non-array)
environment variables in the container you're running, or overwrite variables

</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">VAR2=value2
</span></span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>When running the command, the Docker CLI client checks the value the variable
has in your local environment and passes it to the container.
If no <code>=</code> is provided and that variable isn't exported in your local
environment, the variable is unset in the container.</p><p>You can also load the environment variables from a file. This file should use
the syntax <code>&lt;variable&gt;=value</code> (which sets the variable to the given value) or
<code>&lt;variable&gt;</code> (which takes the value from the local environment), and <code>#</code> for
comments. Lines beginning with <code>#</code> are treated as line comments and are
ignored, whereas a <code>#</code> appearing anywhere else in a line is treated as part of
the variable value.</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBjYXQgZW52Lmxpc3QKIyBUaGlzIGlzIGEgY29tbWVudApWQVIxPXZhbHVlMQpWQVIyPXZhbHVlMgpVU0VSCgokIGRvY2tlciBydW4gLS1lbnYtZmlsZSBlbnYubGlzdCB1YnVudHUgZW52IHwgZ3JlcCAtRSAnVkFSfFVTRVInClZBUjE9dmFsdWUxClZBUjI9dmFsdWUyClVTRVI9am9uemVvbGxh', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));

</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>The <code>my-label</code> key doesn't specify a value so the label defaults to an empty

overwrites the previous. Docker uses the last <code>key=value</code> you supply.</p><p>Use the <code>--label-file</code> flag to load multiple labels from a file. Delimit each

</span></span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>You can load multiple label-files by supplying multiple <code>--label-file</code> flags.</p><p>For additional information on working with labels, see
<a class="link" href="/config/labels-custom-metadata/">Labels</a>.</p><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="network"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#network">Connect a container to a network (--network)</a></h3><p>To start a container and connect it to a network, use the <code>--network</code> option.</p><p>The following commands create a network named <code>my-net</code> and adds a <code>busybox</code> container
to the <code>my-net</code> network.</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgbmV0d29yayBjcmVhdGUgbXktbmV0CiQgZG9ja2VyIHJ1biAtaXRkIC0tbmV0d29yaz1teS1uZXQgYnVzeWJveA==', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">

<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker network create my-net
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run -itd --network<span class="o">=</span>my-net busybox
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>You can also choose the IP addresses for the container with <code>--ip</code> and <code>--ip6</code>
flags when you start the container on a user-defined network. To assign a
static IP to containers, you must specify subnet block for the network.</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgbmV0d29yayBjcmVhdGUgLS1zdWJuZXQgMTkyLjAuMi4wLzI0IG15LW5ldAokIGRvY2tlciBydW4gLWl0ZCAtLW5ldHdvcms9bXktbmV0IC0taXA9MTkyLjAuMi42OSBidXN5Ym94', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker network create --subnet 192.0.2.0/24 my-net
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run -itd --network<span class="o">=</span>my-net --ip<span class="o">=</span>192.0.2.69 busybox
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>If you want to add a running container to a network use the <code>docker network connect</code> subcommand.</p><p>You can connect multiple containers to the same network. Once connected, the
containers can communicate using only another container's IP address
or name. For <code>overlay</code> networks or custom plugins that support multi-host
connectivity, containers connected to the same multi-host network but launched
from different Engines can also communicate in this way.</p><blockquote><p><strong>Note</strong></p><p>The default bridge network only allow containers to communicate with each other using
internal IP addresses. User-created bridge networks provide DNS resolution between
containers using container names.</p></blockquote><p>You can disconnect a container from a network using the <code>docker network disconnect</code> command.</p><p>For more information on connecting a container to a network when using the <code>run</code> command, see the
<a class="link" href="/network/">"<em>Docker network overview</em>"</a>.</p><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="volumes-from"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#volumes-from">Mount volumes from container (--volumes-from)</a></h3><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC0tdm9sdW1lcy1mcm9tIDc3N2Y3ZGM5MmRhNyAtLXZvbHVtZXMtZnJvbSBiYThjMGM1NGYwZjI6cm8gLWkgLXQgdWJ1bnR1IHB3ZA==', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run --volumes-from 777f7dc92da7 --volumes-from ba8c0c54f0f2:ro -i -t ubuntu <span class="nb">pwd</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>The <code>--volumes-from</code> flag mounts all the defined volumes from the referenced
containers. You can specify more than one container by repetitions of the <code>--volumes-from</code>
argument. The container ID may be optionally suffixed with <code>:ro</code> or <code>:rw</code> to
mount the volumes in read-only or read-write mode, respectively. By default,
Docker mounts the volumes in the same mode (read write or read only) as
the reference container.</p><p>Labeling systems like SELinux require placing proper labels on volume
content mounted into a container. Without a label, the security system might
prevent the processes running inside the container from using the content. By
default, Docker does not change the labels set by the OS.</p><p>To change the label in the container context, you can add either of two suffixes
<code>:z</code> or <code>:Z</code> to the volume mount. These suffixes tell Docker to relabel file
objects on the shared volumes. The <code>z</code> option tells Docker that two containers
share the volume content. As a result, Docker labels the content with a shared
content label. Shared volume labels allow all containers to read/write content.
The <code>Z</code> option tells Docker to label the content with a private unshared label.
Only the current container can use a private volume.</p><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="detach"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#detach">Detached mode (-d, --detach)</a></h3><p>The <code>--detach</code> (or <code>-d</code>) flag starts a container as a background process that
doesn't occupy your terminal window. By design, containers started in detached
mode exit when the root process used to run the container exits, unless you
also specify the <code>--rm</code> option. If you use <code>-d</code> with <code>--rm</code>, the container is
removed when it exits or when the daemon exits, whichever happens first.</p><p>Don't pass a <code>service x start</code> command to a detached container. For example,
this command attempts to start the <code>nginx</code> service.</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC1kIC1wIDgwOjgwIG15X2ltYWdlIHNlcnZpY2Ugbmdpbnggc3RhcnQ=', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run -d -p 80:80 my_image service nginx start
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>This succeeds in starting the <code>nginx</code> service inside the container. However, it
fails the detached container paradigm in that, the root process (<code>service nginx start</code>) returns and the detached container stops as designed. As a result, the
<code>nginx</code> service starts but can't be used. Instead, to start a process such as
the <code>nginx</code> web server do the following:</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC1kIC1wIDgwOjgwIG15X2ltYWdlIG5naW54IC1nICdkYWVtb24gb2ZmOyc=', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run -d -p 80:80 my_image nginx -g <span class="s1">'daemon off;'</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>To do input/output with a detached container use network connections or shared
volumes. These are required because the container is no longer listening to the
command line where <code>docker run</code> was run.</p><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="detach-keys"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#detach-keys">Override the detach sequence (--detach-keys)</a></h3><p>Use the <code>--detach-keys</code> option to override the Docker key sequence for detach.
This is useful if the Docker default sequence conflicts with key sequence you
use for other applications. There are two ways to define your own detach key
sequence, as a per-container override or as a configuration property on your
entire configuration.</p><p>To override the sequence for an individual container, use the
<code>--detach-keys="&lt;sequence&gt;"</code> flag with the <code>docker attach</code> command. The format of
the <code>&lt;sequence&gt;</code> is either a letter [a-Z], or the <code>ctrl-</code> combined with any of
the following:</p><ul><li><code>a-z</code> (a single lowercase alpha character )</li><li><code>@</code> (at sign)</li><li><code>[</code> (left bracket)</li><li><code>\\</code> (two backward slashes)</li><li><code>_</code> (underscore)</li><li><code>^</code> (caret)</li></ul><p>These <code>a</code>, <code>ctrl-a</code>, <code>X</code>, or <code>ctrl-\\</code> values are all examples of valid key
sequences. To configure a different configuration default key sequence for all
containers, see
<a class="link" href="/engine/reference/commandline/cli/#configuration-files"><strong>Configuration file</strong> section</a>.</p><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="device"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#device">Add host device to container (--device)</a></h3><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC1pdCAtLXJtIFwKICAgIC0tZGV2aWNlPS9kZXYvc2RjOi9kZXYveHZkYyBcCiAgICAtLWRldmljZT0vZGV2L3NkZCBcCiAgICAtLWRldmljZT0vZGV2L3plcm86L2Rldi9mb29iYXIgXAogICAgdWJ1bnR1IGxzIC1sIC9kZXYve3h2ZGMsc2RkLGZvb2Jhcn0KCmJydy1ydy0tLS0gMSByb290IGRpc2sgOCwgMiBGZWIgIDkgMTY6MDUgL2Rldi94dmRjCmJydy1ydy0tLS0gMSByb290IGRpc2sgOCwgMyBGZWIgIDkgMTY6MDUgL2Rldi9zZGQKY3J3LXJ3LXJ3LSAxIHJvb3Qgcm9vdCAxLCA1IEZlYiAgOSAxNjowNSAvZGV2L2Zvb2Jhcg==', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run -it --rm <span class="se">\
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="se"></span><span class="go">    --device=/dev/sdc:/dev/xvdc \
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">    --device=/dev/sdd \
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">    --device=/dev/zero:/dev/foobar \
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">    ubuntu ls -l /dev/{xvdc,sdd,foobar}
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go"></span><span class="err">
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="err"></span><span class="go">brw-rw---- 1 root disk 8, 2 Feb  9 16:05 /dev/xvdc
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">brw-rw---- 1 root disk 8, 3 Feb  9 16:05 /dev/sdd
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">crw-rw-rw- 1 root root 1, 5 Feb  9 16:05 /dev/foobar
</span></span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>It's often necessary to directly expose devices to a container. The <code>--device</code>
option enables that. For example, adding a specific block storage device or loop
device or audio device to an otherwise unprivileged container
(without the <code>--privileged</code> flag) and have the application directly access it.</p><p>By default, the container is able to <code>read</code>, <code>write</code> and <code>mknod</code> these devices.
This can be overridden using a third <code>:rwm</code> set of options to each <code>--device</code>
flag. If the container is running in privileged mode, then Docker ignores the
specified permissions.</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC0tZGV2aWNlPS9kZXYvc2RhOi9kZXYveHZkYyAtLXJtIC1pdCB1YnVudHUgZmRpc2sgIC9kZXYveHZkYwoKQ29tbWFuZCAobSBmb3IgaGVscCk6IHEKJCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC0tZGV2aWNlPS9kZXYvc2RhOi9kZXYveHZkYzpyIC0tcm0gLWl0IHVidW50dSBmZGlzayAgL2Rldi94dmRjCllvdSB3aWxsIG5vdCBiZSBhYmxlIHRvIHdyaXRlIHRoZSBwYXJ0aXRpb24gdGFibGUuCgpDb21tYW5kIChtIGZvciBoZWxwKTogcQoKJCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC0tZGV2aWNlPS9kZXYvc2RhOi9kZXYveHZkYzpydyAtLXJtIC1pdCB1YnVudHUgZmRpc2sgIC9kZXYveHZkYwoKQ29tbWFuZCAobSBmb3IgaGVscCk6IHEKCiQgZG9ja2VyIHJ1biAtLWRldmljZT0vZGV2L3NkYTovZGV2L3h2ZGM6bSAtLXJtIC1pdCB1YnVudHUgZmRpc2sgIC9kZXYveHZkYwpmZGlzazogdW5hYmxlIHRvIG9wZW4gL2Rldi94dmRjOiBPcGVyYXRpb24gbm90IHBlcm1pdHRlZA==', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));

      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run --device<span class="o">=</span>/dev/sda:/dev/xvdc --rm -it ubuntu fdisk  /dev/xvdc
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="err">
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="err"></span><span class="go">Command (m for help): q
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go"></span><span class="gp">$</span> docker run --device<span class="o">=</span>/dev/sda:/dev/xvdc:r --rm -it ubuntu fdisk  /dev/xvdc
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">You will not be able to write the partition table.
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go"></span><span class="err">
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="err"></span><span class="go">Command (m for help): q
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go"></span><span class="err">
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="err"></span><span class="gp">$</span> docker run --device<span class="o">=</span>/dev/sda:/dev/xvdc:rw --rm -it ubuntu fdisk  /dev/xvdc
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="err">
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="err"></span><span class="go">Command (m for help): q
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go"></span><span class="err">
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="err"></span><span class="gp">$</span> docker run --device<span class="o">=</span>/dev/sda:/dev/xvdc:m --rm -it ubuntu fdisk  /dev/xvdc
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">fdisk: unable to open /dev/xvdc: Operation not permitted
</span></span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><blockquote><p><strong>Note</strong></p><p>The <code>--device</code> option cannot be safely used with ephemeral devices. You shouldn't
add block devices that may be removed to untrusted containers with <code>--device</code>.</p></blockquote><p>For Windows, the format of the string passed to the <code>--device</code> option is in
the form of <code>--device=&lt;IdType&gt;/&lt;Id&gt;</code>. Beginning with Windows Server 2019
and Windows 10 October 2018 Update, Windows only supports an IdType of
<code>class</code> and the Id as a
<a class="link" href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/windows-hardware/drivers/install/overview-of-device-interface-classes" target="_blank" rel="noopener">device interface class
GUID<span class="pl-1 icon-svg icon-sm"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M180-120q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-6e2q0-24 18-42t42-18h249q12.75.0 21.375 8.675 8.625 8.676 8.625 21.5.0 12.825-8.625 21.325T429-780H180v6e2h6e2v-249q0-12.75 8.675-21.375 8.676-8.625 21.5-8.625 12.825.0 21.325 8.625T840-429v249q0 24-18 42t-42 18H180zm6e2-617L403-360q-9 9-21 8.5t-21-9.5-9-21 9-21l377-377H549q-12.75.0-21.375-8.675-8.625-8.676-8.625-21.5.0-12.825 8.625-21.325T549-840h291v291q0 12.75-8.675 21.375-8.676 8.625-21.5 8.625-12.825.0-21.325-8.625T780-549v-188z"></path></svg></span></a>.
Refer to the table defined in the
<a class="link" href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/virtualization/windowscontainers/deploy-containers/hardware-devices-in-containers" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Windows container
docs<span class="pl-1 icon-svg icon-sm"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M180-120q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-6e2q0-24 18-42t42-18h249q12.75.0 21.375 8.675 8.625 8.676 8.625 21.5.0 12.825-8.625 21.325T429-780H180v6e2h6e2v-249q0-12.75 8.675-21.375 8.676-8.625 21.5-8.625 12.825.0 21.325 8.625T840-429v249q0 24-18 42t-42 18H180zm6e2-617L403-360q-9 9-21 8.5t-21-9.5-9-21 9-21l377-377H549q-12.75.0-21.375-8.675-8.625-8.676-8.625-21.5.0-12.825 8.625-21.325T549-840h291v291q0 12.75-8.675 21.375-8.676 8.625-21.5 8.625-12.825.0-21.325-8.625T780-549v-188z"></path></svg></span></a>
for a list of container-supported device interface class GUIDs.</p><p>If you specify this option for a process-isolated Windows container, Docker makes
<em>all</em> devices that implement the requested device interface class GUID
available in the container. For example, the command below makes all COM

and produces an error if the container isolation is <code>hyperv</code>.</p></blockquote><h4 class="scroll-mt-20" id="cdi-devices"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#cdi-devices">CDI devices</a></h4><blockquote><p><strong>Note</strong></p><p>This is experimental feature and as such doesn't represent a stable API.</p></blockquote><p>Container Device Interface (CDI) is a
<a class="link" href="https://github.com/cncf-tags/container-device-interface/blob/main/SPEC.md" target="_blank" rel="noopener">standardized<span class="pl-1 icon-svg icon-sm"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M180-120q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-6e2q0-24 18-42t42-18h249q12.75.0 21.375 8.675 8.625 8.676 8.625 21.5.0 12.825-8.625 21.325T429-780H180v6e2h6e2v-249q0-12.75 8.675-21.375 8.676-8.625 21.5-8.625 12.825.0 21.325 8.625T840-429v249q0 24-18 42t-42 18H180zm6e2-617L403-360q-9 9-21 8.5t-21-9.5-9-21 9-21l377-377H549q-12.75.0-21.375-8.675-8.625-8.676-8.625-21.5.0-12.825 8.625-21.325T549-840h291v291q0 12.75-8.675 21.375-8.676 8.625-21.5 8.625-12.825.0-21.325-8.625T780-549v-188z"></path></svg></span></a>
mechanism for container runtimes to create containers which are able to
interact with third party devices.</p><p>With CDI, device configurations are defined using a JSON file. In addition to
enabling the container to interact with the device node, it also lets you
specify additional configuration for the device, such as kernel modules, host
libraries, and environment variables.</p><p>You can reference a CDI device with the <code>--device</code> flag using the
fully-qualified name of the device, as shown in the following example:</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC0tZGV2aWNlPXZlbmRvci5jb20vY2xhc3M9ZGV2aWNlLW5hbWUgLS1ybSAtaXQgdWJ1bnR1', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run --device<span class="o">=</span>vendor.com/class<span class="o">=</span>device-name --rm -it ubuntu
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>This starts an <code>ubuntu</code> container with access to the specified CDI device,
<code>vendor.com/class=device-name</code>, assuming that:</p><ul><li>A valid CDI specification (JSON file) for the requested device is available
on the system running the daemon, in one of the configured CDI specification
directories.</li><li>The CDI feature has been enabled on the daemon side, see
<a class="link" href="/reference/cli/dockerd/#enable-cdi-devices">Enable CDI
devices</a>.</li></ul><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="attach"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#attach">Attach to STDIN/STDOUT/STDERR (-a, --attach)</a></h3><p>The <code>--attach</code> (or <code>-a</code>) flag tells <code>docker run</code> to bind to the container's
<code>STDIN</code>, <code>STDOUT</code> or <code>STDERR</code>. This makes it possible to manipulate the output
and input as needed. You can specify to which of the three standard streams

      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
