</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><blockquote><p><strong>Note</strong></p><p>A process running as PID 1 inside a container is treated specially by
Linux: it ignores any signal with the default action. So, the process
doesn't terminate on <code>SIGINT</code> or <code>SIGTERM</code> unless it's coded to do so.</p></blockquote><p>See also
<a class="link" href="/reference/cli/docker/container/cp/">the <code>docker cp</code> command</a>.</p><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="interactive"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#interactive">Keep STDIN open (-i, --interactive)</a></h3><p>The <code>--interactive</code> (or <code>-i</code>) flag keeps the container's <code>STDIN</code> open, and lets
you send input to the container through standard input.</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBlY2hvIGhlbGxvIHwgZG9ja2VyIHJ1biAtLXJtIC1pIGJ1c3lib3ggY2F0CmhlbGxv', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>

</span></span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>The <code>-i</code> flag is most often used together with the <code>--tty</code> flag to bind the I/O
streams of the container to a pseudo terminal, creating an interactive terminal
session for the container. See

</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">rab
</span></span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="init"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#init">Specify an init process</a></h3><p>You can use the <code>--init</code> flag to indicate that an init process should be used as
the PID 1 in the container. Specifying an init process ensures the usual
responsibilities of an init system, such as reaping zombie processes, are
performed inside the created container.</p><p>The default init process used is the first <code>docker-init</code> executable found in the
system path of the Docker daemon process. This <code>docker-init</code> binary, included in
the default installation, is backed by
<a class="link" href="https://github.com/krallin/tini" target="_blank" rel="noopener">tini<span class="pl-1 icon-svg icon-sm"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M180-120q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-6e2q0-24 18-42t42-18h249q12.75.0 21.375 8.675 8.625 8.676 8.625 21.5.0 12.825-8.625 21.325T429-780H180v6e2h6e2v-249q0-12.75 8.675-21.375 8.676-8.625 21.5-8.625 12.825.0 21.325 8.625T840-429v249q0 24-18 42t-42 18H180zm6e2-617L403-360q-9 9-21 8.5t-21-9.5-9-21 9-21l377-377H549q-12.75.0-21.375-8.675-8.625-8.676-8.625-21.5.0-12.825 8.625-21.325T549-840h291v291q0 12.75-8.675 21.375-8.676 8.625-21.5 8.625-12.825.0-21.325-8.625T780-549v-188z"></path></svg></span></a>.</p><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="tty"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#tty">Allocate a pseudo-TTY (-t, --tty)</a></h3><p>The <code>--tty</code> (or <code>-t</code>) flag attaches a pseudo-TTY to the container, connecting
your terminal to the I/O streams of the container. Allocating a pseudo-TTY to
the container means that you get access to input and output feature that TTY
devices provide.</p><p>For example, the following command runs the <code>passwd</code> command in a <code>debian</code>
container, to set a new password for the <code>root</code> user.</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC1pIGRlYmlhbiBwYXNzd2Qgcm9vdApOZXcgcGFzc3dvcmQ6IGthcmphbGFucGlpcmFra2E5ClJldHlwZSBuZXcgcGFzc3dvcmQ6IGthcmphbGFucGlpcmFra2E5CnBhc3N3ZDogcGFzc3dvcmQgdXBkYXRlZCBzdWNjZXNzZnVsbHk=', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run -i debian passwd root
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">New password: karjalanpiirakka9
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">Retype new password: karjalanpiirakka9
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">passwd: password updated successfully
</span></span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>If you run this command with only the <code>-i</code> flag (which lets you send text to
<code>STDIN</code> of the container), the <code>passwd</code> prompt displays the password in plain
text. However, if you try the same thing but also adding the <code>-t</code> flag, the
password is hidden:</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC1pdCBkZWJpYW4gcGFzc3dkIHJvb3QKTmV3IHBhc3N3b3JkOgpSZXR5cGUgbmV3IHBhc3N3b3JkOgpwYXNzd2Q6IHBhc3N3b3JkIHVwZGF0ZWQgc3VjY2Vzc2Z1bGx5', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run -it debian passwd root
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">New password:
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">Retype new password:
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">passwd: password updated successfully
</span></span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>This is because <code>passwd</code> can suppress the output of characters to the terminal
using the echo-off TTY feature.</p><p>You can use the <code>-t</code> flag without <code>-i</code> flag. This still allocates a pseudo-TTY
to the container, but with no way of writing to <code>STDIN</code>. The only time this
might be useful is if the output of the container requires a TTY environment.</p><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="cgroup-parent"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#cgroup-parent">Specify custom cgroups</a></h3><p>Using the <code>--cgroup-parent</code> flag, you can pass a specific cgroup to run a
container in. This allows you to create and manage cgroups on their own. You can
define custom resources for those cgroups and put containers under a common
parent group.</p><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="device-cgroup-rule"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#device-cgroup-rule">Using dynamically created devices (--device-cgroup-rule)</a></h3><p>Docker assigns devices available to a container at creation time. The
assigned devices are added to the cgroup.allow file and
created into the container when it runs. This poses a problem when
you need to add a new device to running container.</p><p>One solution is to add a more permissive rule to a container
allowing it access to a wider range of devices. For example, supposing
the container needs access to a character device with major <code>42</code> and
any number of minor numbers (added as new devices appear), add the
following rule:</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC1kIC0tZGV2aWNlLWNncm91cC1ydWxlPSdjIDQyOiogcm13JyAtLW5hbWUgbXktY29udGFpbmVyIG15LWltYWdl', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run -d --device-cgroup-rule<span class="o">=</span><span class="s1">'c 42:* rmw'</span> --name my-container my-image
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>Then, a user could ask <code>udev</code> to execute a script that would <code>docker exec my-container mknod newDevX c 42 &lt;minor&gt;</code>
the required device when it is added.</p><blockquote><p><strong>Note</strong>: You still need to explicitly add initially present devices to the
<code>docker run</code> / <code>docker create</code> command.</p></blockquote><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="gpus"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#gpus">Access an NVIDIA GPU</a></h3><p>The <code>--gpus</code> flag allows you to access NVIDIA GPU resources. First you need to
install the
<a class="link" href="https://nvidia.github.io/nvidia-container-runtime/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">nvidia-container-runtime<span class="pl-1 icon-svg icon-sm"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M180-120q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-6e2q0-24 18-42t42-18h249q12.75.0 21.375 8.675 8.625 8.676 8.625 21.5.0 12.825-8.625 21.325T429-780H180v6e2h6e2v-249q0-12.75 8.675-21.375 8.676-8.625 21.5-8.625 12.825.0 21.325 8.625T840-429v249q0 24-18 42t-42 18H180zm6e2-617L403-360q-9 9-21 8.5t-21-9.5-9-21 9-21l377-377H549q-12.75.0-21.375-8.675-8.625-8.676-8.625-21.5.0-12.825 8.625-21.325T549-840h291v291q0 12.75-8.675 21.375-8.676 8.625-21.5 8.625-12.825.0-21.325-8.625T780-549v-188z"></path></svg></span></a>.</p><blockquote><p><strong>Note</strong></p><p>You can also specify a GPU as a CDI device with the <code>--device</code> flag, see
<a class="link" href="#cdi-devices">CDI devices</a>.</p></blockquote><p>Read
<a class="link" href="/config/containers/resource_constraints/">Specify a container's resources</a>
for more information.</p><p>To use <code>--gpus</code>, specify which GPUs (or all) to use. If you provide no value, Docker uses all
available GPUs. The example below exposes all available GPUs.</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC1pdCAtLXJtIC0tZ3B1cyBhbGwgdWJ1bnR1IG52aWRpYS1zbWk=', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run -it --rm --gpus all ubuntu nvidia-smi
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>Use the <code>device</code> option to specify GPUs. The example below exposes a specific
GPU.</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC1pdCAtLXJtIC0tZ3B1cyBkZXZpY2U9R1BVLTNhMjNjNjY5LTFmNjktYzY0ZS1jZjg1LTQ0ZTliMDdlN2EyYSB1YnVudHUgbnZpZGlhLXNtaQ==', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>

</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>The example below exposes the first and third GPUs.</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC1pdCAtLXJtIC0tZ3B1cyAnImRldmljZT0wLDIiJyB1YnVudHUgbnZpZGlhLXNtaQ==', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));

      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run -it --rm --gpus <span class="s1">'"device=0,2"'</span> ubuntu nvidia-smi
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="restart"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#restart">Restart policies (--restart)</a></h3><p>Use the <code>--restart</code> flag to specify a container's <em>restart policy</em>. A restart
policy controls whether the Docker daemon restarts a container after exit.
Docker supports the following restart policies:</p><table><thead><tr><th style="text-align:left">Policy</th><th style="text-align:left">Result</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td style="text-align:left"><code>no</code></td><td style="text-align:left">Do not automatically restart the container when it exits. This is the default.</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:left"><code>on-failure[:max-retries]</code></td><td style="text-align:left">Restart only if the container exits with a non-zero exit status. Optionally, limit the number of restart retries the Docker daemon attempts.</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:left"><code>unless-stopped</code></td><td style="text-align:left">Restart the container unless it's explicitly stopped or Docker itself is stopped or restarted.</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:left"><code>always</code></td><td style="text-align:left">Always restart the container regardless of the exit status. When you specify always, the Docker daemon tries to restart the container indefinitely. The container always starts on daemon startup, regardless of the current state of the container.</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC0tcmVzdGFydD1hbHdheXMgcmVkaXM=', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run --restart<span class="o">=</span>always redis
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>This runs the <code>redis</code> container with a restart policy of <strong>always</strong>.
If the container exits, Docker restarts it.</p><p>When a restart policy is active on a container, it shows as either <code>Up</code> or
<code>Restarting</code> in
<a class="link" href="/reference/cli/docker/container/ls/"><code>docker ps</code></a>. It can also be useful to use
<a class="link" href="/reference/cli/docker/system/events/"><code>docker events</code></a> to see the restart policy in effect.</p><p>An increasing delay (double the previous delay, starting at 100 milliseconds)
is added before each restart to prevent flooding the server. This means the
daemon waits for 100 ms, then 200 ms, 400, 800, 1600, and so on until either
the <code>on-failure</code> limit, the maximum delay of 1 minute is hit, or when you
<code>docker stop</code> or <code>docker rm -f</code> the container.</p><p>If a container is successfully restarted (the container is started and runs
for at least 10 seconds), the delay is reset to its default value of 100 ms.</p><h4 class="scroll-mt-20" id="specify-a-limit-for-restart-attempts"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#specify-a-limit-for-restart-attempts">Specify a limit for restart attempts</a></h4><p>You can specify the maximum amount of times Docker attempts to restart the
container when using the <strong>on-failure</strong> policy. By default, Docker never stops
attempting to restart the container.</p><p>The following example runs the <code>redis</code> container with a restart policy of
<strong>on-failure</strong> and a maximum restart count of 10.</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC0tcmVzdGFydD1vbi1mYWlsdXJlOjEwIHJlZGlz', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run --restart<span class="o">=</span>on-failure:10 redis
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>If the <code>redis</code> container exits with a non-zero exit status more than 10 times
in a row, Docker stops trying to restart the container. Providing a maximum
restart limit is only valid for the <strong>on-failure</strong> policy.</p><h4 class="scroll-mt-20" id="inspect-container-restarts"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#inspect-container-restarts">Inspect container restarts</a></h4><p>The number of (attempted) restarts for a container can be obtained using the
<a class="link" href="/reference/cli/docker/inspect/"><code>docker inspect</code></a> command. For example, to get the number of
restarts for container "my-container";</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgaW5zcGVjdCAtZiAie3sgLlJlc3RhcnRDb3VudCB9fSIgbXktY29udGFpbmVyCjI=', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker inspect -f <span class="s2">"{{ .RestartCount }}"</span> my-container

<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker inspect -f <span class="s2">"{{ .State.StartedAt }}"</span> my-container
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">2015-03-04T23:47:07.691840179Z
</span></span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>Combining <code>--restart</code> (restart policy) with the <code>--rm</code> (clean up) flag results
in an error. On container restart, attached clients are disconnected.</p><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="rm"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#rm">Clean up (--rm)</a></h3><p>By default, a container's file system persists even after the container exits.
This makes debugging a lot easier, since you can inspect the container's final
state and you retain all your data.</p><p>If you are running short-term <strong>foreground</strong> processes, these container file
systems can start to pile up. If you'd like Docker to automatically clean up
the container and remove the file system when the container exits, use the
<code>--rm</code> flag:</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'LS1ybT1mYWxzZTogQXV0b21hdGljYWxseSByZW1vdmUgdGhlIGNvbnRhaW5lciB3aGVuIGl0IGV4aXRz', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-text" data-lang="text"><span class="line"><span class="cl">--rm=false: Automatically remove the container when it exits</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><blockquote><p><strong>Note</strong></p><p>If you set the <code>--rm</code> flag, Docker also removes the anonymous volumes
associated with the container when the container is removed. This is similar
to running <code>docker rm -v my-container</code>. Only volumes that are specified
without a name are removed. For example, when running the following command,
volume <code>/foo</code> is removed, but not <code>/bar</code>:</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC0tcm0gLXYgL2ZvbyAtdiBhd2Vzb21lOi9iYXIgYnVzeWJveCB0b3A=', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run --rm -v /foo -v awesome:/bar busybox top
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>Volumes inherited via <code>--volumes-from</code> are removed with the same logic:
if the original volume was specified with a name it isn't removed.</p></blockquote><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="add-host"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#add-host">Add entries to container hosts file (--add-host)</a></h3><p>You can add other hosts into a container's <code>/etc/hosts</code> file by using one or
more <code>--add-host</code> flags. This example adds a static address for a host named
<code>my-hostname</code>:</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC0tYWRkLWhvc3Q9bXktaG9zdG5hbWU9OC44LjguOCAtLXJtIC1pdCBhbHBpbmUKCi8gIyBwaW5nIG15LWhvc3RuYW1lClBJTkcgbXktaG9zdG5hbWUgKDguOC44LjgpOiA1NiBkYXRhIGJ5dGVzCjY0IGJ5dGVzIGZyb20gOC44LjguODogc2VxPTAgdHRsPTM3IHRpbWU9OTMuMDUyIG1zCjY0IGJ5dGVzIGZyb20gOC44LjguODogc2VxPTEgdHRsPTM3IHRpbWU9OTIuNDY3IG1zCjY0IGJ5dGVzIGZyb20gOC44LjguODogc2VxPTIgdHRsPTM3IHRpbWU9OTIuMjUyIG1zCl5DCi0tLSBteS1ob3N0bmFtZSBwaW5nIHN0YXRpc3RpY3MgLS0tCjQgcGFja2V0cyB0cmFuc21pdHRlZCwgNCBwYWNrZXRzIHJlY2VpdmVkLCAwJSBwYWNrZXQgbG9zcwpyb3VuZC10cmlwIG1pbi9hdmcvbWF4ID0gOTIuMjA5LzkyLjQ5NS85My4wNTIgbXM=', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">

</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>The <code>--add-host</code> flag supports a special <code>host-gateway</code> value that resolves to
the internal IP address of the host. This is useful when you want containers to
connect to services running on the host machine.</p><p>It's conventional to use <code>host.docker.internal</code> as the hostname referring to
<code>host-gateway</code>. Docker Desktop automatically resolves this hostname, see
<a class="link" href="/desktop/networking/#i-want-to-connect-from-a-container-to-a-service-on-the-host">Explore networking features</a>.</p><p>The following example shows how the special <code>host-gateway</code> value works. The
example runs an HTTP server that serves a file from host to container over the
<code>host.docker.internal</code> hostname, which resolves to the host's internal IP.</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBlY2hvICJoZWxsbyBmcm9tIGhvc3QhIiA+IC4vaGVsbG8KJCBweXRob24zIC1tIGh0dHAuc2VydmVyIDgwMDAKU2VydmluZyBIVFRQIG9uIDAuMC4wLjAgcG9ydCA4MDAwIChodHRwOi8vMC4wLjAuMDo4MDAwLykgLi4uCiQgZG9ja2VyIHJ1biBcCiAgLS1hZGQtaG9zdCBob3N0LmRvY2tlci5pbnRlcm5hbD1ob3N0LWdhdGV3YXkgXAogIGN1cmxpbWFnZXMvY3VybCAtcyBob3N0LmRvY2tlci5pbnRlcm5hbDo4MDAwL2hlbGxvCmhlbGxvIGZyb20gaG9zdCE=', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));

</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="log-driver"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#log-driver">Logging drivers (--log-driver)</a></h3><p>The container can have a different logging driver than the Docker daemon. Use
the <code>--log-driver=&lt;DRIVER&gt;</code> with the <code>docker run</code> command to configure the
container's logging driver.</p><p>To learn about the supported logging drivers and how to use them, refer to
<a class="link" href="/config/containers/logging/configure/">Configure logging drivers</a>.</p><p>To disable logging for a container, set the <code>--log-driver</code> flag to <code>none</code>:</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC0tbG9nLWRyaXZlcj1ub25lIC1kIG5naW54OmFscGluZQo1MTAxZDNiN2ZlOTMxYzI3YzJiYTBlNjVmZDk4OTY1NGQyOTczOTNhZDY1YWUyMzhmMjBiOTdhMDIwZTcyOTViCiQgZG9ja2VyIGxvZ3MgNTEwMWQzYgpFcnJvciByZXNwb25zZSBmcm9tIGRhZW1vbjogY29uZmlndXJlZCBsb2dnaW5nIGRyaXZlciBkb2VzIG5vdCBzdXBwb3J0IHJlYWRpbmc=', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">

</span></span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="ulimit"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#ulimit">Set ulimits in container (--ulimit)</a></h3><p>Since setting <code>ulimit</code> settings in a container requires extra privileges not
available in the default container, you can set these using the <code>--ulimit</code> flag.
Specify <code>--ulimit</code> with a soft and hard limit in the format
<code>&lt;type&gt;=&lt;soft limit&gt;[:&lt;hard limit&gt;]</code>. For example:</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC0tdWxpbWl0IG5vZmlsZT0xMDI0OjEwMjQgLS1ybSBkZWJpYW4gc2ggLWMgInVsaW1pdCAtbiIKMTAyNA==', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run --ulimit <span class="nv">nofile</span><span class="o">=</span>1024:1024 --rm debian sh -c <span class="s2">"ulimit -n"</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="go">1024
</span></span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><blockquote><p><strong>Note</strong></p><p>If you don't provide a hard limit value, Docker uses the soft limit value
for both values. If you don't provide any values, they are inherited from
the default <code>ulimits</code> set on the daemon.</p></blockquote><blockquote><p><strong>Note</strong></p><p>The <code>as</code> option is deprecated.

      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">

<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run -it --ulimit <span class="nv">as</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="m">1024</span> fedora /bin/bash
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></blockquote><p>Docker sends the values to the appropriate OS <code>syscall</code> and doesn't perform any byte conversion.
Take this into account when setting the values.</p><h4 class="scroll-mt-20" id="for-nproc-usage"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#for-nproc-usage">For nproc usage</a></h4><p>Be careful setting <code>nproc</code> with the <code>ulimit</code> flag as Linux uses <code>nproc</code> to set the
maximum number of processes available to a user, not to a container. For example, start four
containers with <code>daemon</code> user:</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC1kIC11IGRhZW1vbiAtLXVsaW1pdCBucHJvYz0zIGJ1c3lib3ggdG9wCgokIGRvY2tlciBydW4gLWQgLXUgZGFlbW9uIC0tdWxpbWl0IG5wcm9jPTMgYnVzeWJveCB0b3AKCiQgZG9ja2VyIHJ1biAtZCAtdSBkYWVtb24gLS11bGltaXQgbnByb2M9MyBidXN5Ym94IHRvcAoKJCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC1kIC11IGRhZW1vbiAtLXVsaW1pdCBucHJvYz0zIGJ1c3lib3ggdG9w', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run -d -u daemon --ulimit <span class="nv">nproc</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="m">3</span> busybox top
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="err">
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="err"></span><span class="gp">$</span> docker run -d -u daemon --ulimit <span class="nv">nproc</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="m">3</span> busybox top
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="err">

</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="err">
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="err"></span><span class="gp">$</span> docker run -d -u daemon --ulimit <span class="nv">nproc</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="m">3</span> busybox top
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>The 4th container fails and reports a "[8] System error: resource temporarily unavailable" error.
This fails because the caller set <code>nproc=3</code> resulting in the first three containers using up
the three processes quota set for the <code>daemon</code> user.</p><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="stop-signal"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#stop-signal">Stop container with signal (--stop-signal)</a></h3><p>The <code>--stop-signal</code> flag sends the system call signal to the
container to exit. This signal can be a signal name in the format <code>SIG&lt;NAME&gt;</code>,
for instance <code>SIGKILL</code>, or an unsigned number that matches a position in the
kernel's syscall table, for instance <code>9</code>.</p><p>The default value is defined by
<a class="link" href="/reference/dockerfile/#stopsignal"><code>STOPSIGNAL</code></a>
in the image, or <code>SIGTERM</code> if the image has no <code>STOPSIGNAL</code> defined.</p><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="security-opt"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#security-opt">Optional security options (--security-opt)</a></h3><table><thead><tr><th style="text-align:left">Option</th><th style="text-align:left">Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td style="text-align:left"><code>--security-opt="label=user:USER"</code></td><td style="text-align:left">Set the label user for the container</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:left"><code>--security-opt="label=role:ROLE"</code></td><td style="text-align:left">Set the label role for the container</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:left"><code>--security-opt="label=type:TYPE"</code></td><td style="text-align:left">Set the label type for the container</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:left"><code>--security-opt="label=level:LEVEL"</code></td><td style="text-align:left">Set the label level for the container</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:left"><code>--security-opt="label=disable"</code></td><td style="text-align:left">Turn off label confinement for the container</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:left"><code>--security-opt="apparmor=PROFILE"</code></td><td style="text-align:left">Set the apparmor profile to be applied to the container</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:left"><code>--security-opt="no-new-privileges=true"</code></td><td style="text-align:left">Disable container processes from gaining new privileges</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:left"><code>--security-opt="seccomp=unconfined"</code></td><td style="text-align:left">Turn off seccomp confinement for the container</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:left"><code>--security-opt="seccomp=builtin"</code></td><td style="text-align:left">Use the default (built-in) seccomp profile for the container. This can be used to enable seccomp for a container running on a daemon with a custom default profile set, or with seccomp disabled ("unconfined").</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:left"><code>--security-opt="seccomp=profile.json"</code></td><td style="text-align:left">White-listed syscalls seccomp Json file to be used as a seccomp filter</td></tr></tbody></table><p>The <code>--security-opt</code> flag lets you override the default labeling scheme for a
container. Specifying the level in the following command allows you to share
the same content between containers.</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC0tc2VjdXJpdHktb3B0IGxhYmVsPWxldmVsOnMwOmMxMDAsYzIwMCAtaXQgZmVkb3JhIGJhc2g=', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));

<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run --security-opt no-new-privileges -it ubuntu bash
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>This means that commands that raise privileges such as <code>su</code> or <code>sudo</code> no longer work.
It also causes any seccomp filters to be applied later, after privileges have been dropped
which may mean you can have a more restrictive set of filters.
For more details, see the
<a class="link" href="https://www.kernel.org/doc/Documentation/prctl/no_new_privs.txt" target="_blank" rel="noopener">kernel documentation<span class="pl-1 icon-svg icon-sm"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M180-120q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-6e2q0-24 18-42t42-18h249q12.75.0 21.375 8.675 8.625 8.676 8.625 21.5.0 12.825-8.625 21.325T429-780H180v6e2h6e2v-249q0-12.75 8.675-21.375 8.676-8.625 21.5-8.625 12.825.0 21.325 8.625T840-429v249q0 24-18 42t-42 18H180zm6e2-617L403-360q-9 9-21 8.5t-21-9.5-9-21 9-21l377-377H549q-12.75.0-21.375-8.675-8.625-8.676-8.625-21.5.0-12.825 8.625-21.325T549-840h291v291q0 12.75-8.675 21.375-8.676 8.625-21.5 8.625-12.825.0-21.325-8.625T780-549v-188z"></path></svg></span></a>.</p><p>On Windows, you can use the <code>--security-opt</code> flag to specify the <code>credentialspec</code> option.
The <code>credentialspec</code> must be in the format <code>file://spec.txt</code> or <code>registry://keyname</code>.</p><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="stop-timeout"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#stop-timeout">Stop container with timeout (--stop-timeout)</a></h3><p>The <code>--stop-timeout</code> flag sets the number of seconds to wait for the container
to stop after sending the pre-defined (see <code>--stop-signal</code>) system call signal.
If the container does not exit after the timeout elapses, it's forcibly killed
with a <code>SIGKILL</code> signal.</p><p>If you set <code>--stop-timeout</code> to <code>-1</code>, no timeout is applied, and the daemon
waits indefinitely for the container to exit.</p><p>The Daemon determines the default, and is 10 seconds for Linux containers,
and 30 seconds for Windows containers.</p><h3 class="scroll-mt-20" id="isolation"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#isolation">Specify isolation technology for container (--isolation)</a></h3><p>This option is useful in situations where you are running Docker containers on
Windows. The <code>--isolation=&lt;value&gt;</code> option sets a container's isolation technology.
On Linux, the only supported is the <code>default</code> option which uses Linux namespaces.
These two commands are equivalent on Linux:</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC1kIGJ1c3lib3ggdG9wCiQgZG9ja2VyIHJ1biAtZCAtLWlzb2xhdGlvbiBkZWZhdWx0IGJ1c3lib3ggdG9w', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">

<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run -d busybox top
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run -d --isolation default busybox top
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><p>On Windows, <code>--isolation</code> can take one of these values:</p><table><thead><tr><th style="text-align:left">Value</th><th style="text-align:left">Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td style="text-align:left"><code>default</code></td><td style="text-align:left">Use the value specified by the Docker daemon's <code>--exec-opt</code> or system default (see below).</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:left"><code>process</code></td><td style="text-align:left">Shared-kernel namespace isolation.</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:left"><code>hyperv</code></td><td style="text-align:left">Hyper-V hypervisor partition-based isolation.</td></tr></tbody></table><p>The default isolation on Windows server operating systems is <code>process</code>, and <code>hyperv</code>
on Windows client operating systems, such as Windows 10. Process isolation has better
performance, but requires that the image and host use the same kernel version.</p><p>On Windows server, assuming the default configuration, these commands are equivalent
and result in <code>process</code> isolation:</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'UFMgQzpcPiBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC1kIG1pY3Jvc29mdC9uYW5vc2VydmVyIHBvd2Vyc2hlbGwgZWNobyBwcm9jZXNzClBTIEM6XD4gZG9ja2VyIHJ1biAtZCAtLWlzb2xhdGlvbiBkZWZhdWx0IG1pY3Jvc29mdC9uYW5vc2VydmVyIHBvd2Vyc2hlbGwgZWNobyBwcm9jZXNzClBTIEM6XD4gZG9ja2VyIHJ1biAtZCAtLWlzb2xhdGlvbiBwcm9jZXNzIG1pY3Jvc29mdC9uYW5vc2VydmVyIHBvd2Vyc2hlbGwgZWNobyBwcm9jZXNz', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">

Linux sets this
on the cgroup and applications in a container can query it at <code>/sys/fs/cgroup/memory/memory.limit_in_bytes</code>.</p><p>On Windows, this affects containers differently depending on what type of isolation you use.</p><ul><li><p>With <code>process</code> isolation, Windows reports the full memory of the host system, not the limit to applications running inside the container</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'UFMgQzpcPiBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC1pdCAtbSAyR0IgLS1pc29sYXRpb249cHJvY2VzcyBtaWNyb3NvZnQvbmFub3NlcnZlciBwb3dlcnNoZWxsIEdldC1Db21wdXRlckluZm8gKm1lbW9yeSoKCkNzVG90YWxQaHlzaWNhbE1lbW9yeSAgICAgIDogMTcwNjQ1MDk0NDAKQ3NQaHlpY2FsbHlJbnN0YWxsZWRNZW1vcnkgOiAxNjc3NzIxNgpPc1RvdGFsVmlzaWJsZU1lbW9yeVNpemUgICA6IDE2NjY0NTYwCk9zRnJlZVBoeXNpY2FsTWVtb3J5ICAgICAgIDogMTQ2NDY3MjAKT3NUb3RhbFZpcnR1YWxNZW1vcnlTaXplICAgOiAxOTE1NDkyOApPc0ZyZWVWaXJ0dWFsTWVtb3J5ICAgICAgICA6IDE3MTk3NDQwCk9zSW5Vc2VWaXJ0dWFsTWVtb3J5ICAgICAgIDogMTk1NzQ4OApPc01heFByb2Nlc3NNZW1vcnlTaXplICAgICA6IDEzNzQzODk1MzM0NA==', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));

container. For example, to turn on IP forwarding in the containers
network namespace, run this command:</p><div class="scroll-mt-20" x-data="" x-ref="root"><div class="group relative"><button x-data="{ code: 'JCBkb2NrZXIgcnVuIC0tc3lzY3RsIG5ldC5pcHY0LmlwX2ZvcndhcmQ9MSBzb21laW1hZ2U=', copying: false }" class="absolute right-3 top-3 z-20 text-gray-light-300 dark:text-gray-dark-600" title="copy" @click="window.navigator.clipboard.writeText(atob(code).replaceAll(/^[\$>]\s+/gm, ''));
      copying = true;
      setTimeout(() => copying = false, 2000);">
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : !copying }" class="icon-svg hidden group-hover:block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="M3e2-2e2q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-560q0-24 18-42t42-18h440q24 0 42 18t18 42v560q0 24-18 42t-42 18H3e2zM180-80q-24 0-42-18t-18-42v-590q0-13 8.5-21.5T150-760t21.5 8.5T180-730v590h470q13 0 21.5 8.5T680-110t-8.5 21.5T650-80H180z"></path></svg></span>
<span :class="{ 'group-hover:block' : copying }" class="icon-svg hidden"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 -960 960 960"><path d="m421-389-98-98q-9-9-22-9t-23 10q-9 9-9 22t9 22l122 123q9 9 21 9t21-9l239-239q10-10 10-23t-10-23q-10-9-23.5-8.5T635-603L421-389zm59 309q-82 0-155-31.5t-127.5-86-86-127.5T80-480q0-83 31.5-156t86-127T325-848.5 480-880q83 0 156 31.5T763-763t85.5 127T880-480q0 82-31.5 155T763-197.5t-127 86T480-80z"></path></svg></span></button><div class="syntax-light dark:syntax-dark"><div class="highlight"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code class="language-console" data-lang="console"><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="gp">$</span> docker run --sysctl net.ipv4.ip_forward<span class="o">=</span><span class="m">1</span> someimage
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><blockquote><p><strong>Note</strong></p><p>Not all sysctls are namespaced. Docker does not support changing sysctls
inside of a container that also modify the host system. As the kernel
evolves we expect to see more sysctls become namespaced.</p></blockquote><h4 class="scroll-mt-20" id="currently-supported-sysctls"><a class="text-black dark:text-white no-underline hover:underline" href="#currently-supported-sysctls">Currently supported sysctls</a></h4><p>IPC Namespace:</p><ul><li><code>kernel.msgmax</code>, <code>kernel.msgmnb</code>, <code>kernel.msgmni</code>, <code>kernel.sem</code>,
<code>kernel.shmall</code>, <code>kernel.shmmax</code>, <code>kernel.shmmni</code>, <code>kernel.shm_rmid_forced</code>.</li><li>Sysctls beginning with <code>fs.mqueue.*</code></li><li>If you use the <code>--ipc=host</code> option these sysctls are not allowed.</li></ul><p>Network Namespace:</p><ul><li>Sysctls beginning with <code>net.*</code></li><li>If you use the <code>--network=host</code> option using these sysctls are not allowed.</li></ul>
